<user>115392272214868184116</user><Name>Avery Salazar<//Name><Time>1618028588546< /Time><rate>5<//rate>< text>
El Buen Cacao served me what was quite possibly the greatest milkshake of my life. The Ghost shake is made with their ghost pepper chocolate and had the perfect amount of spice, for my taste. My husband and I had to order a second one it was such a transcendental experience. I think they really shine in their drink selections here, but their individual chocolates were delicious, pure and beautiful. I tried the pistachio, peanut butter and fig. All supporting roles to the star; that beautiful chocolate. The staff was very friendly, helpful and knowledgeable. They created a wonderful environment in which to enjoy a wonderful food experience. I cannot wait to go back.</text>

<date>1609530751369</date><rate>5</rate>< review>
What a gem. I am going to crave the Mexican hot chocolate when we leave! Idyllwild in general does not have the highest level of cuisine, but this place really stands out as outstanding (I also love Ferro, which uses their chocolate in an amazing gluten-free chocolate cake!). I highly recommend the Mexican hot chocolate, and they have non-dairy milk options, including Oat milk! Very progressive of them in this beautiful mountain town! We will go here every day while we are in town! Great for anyone with gluten allergies or milk allergies!<//review>

WOW-

First - this little girl, literally knee-high, who looks like she could be a Disney character told me the store was closed and I couldn't go in. I asked her what time they closed and she said "30", being that it was 4:40, I assumed they closed. Then my wife tried to go in and she said "No, you can't go in there" we went in anyway and were met with the smell of chocolate... GOOD chocolate and a smiling, grown up version of the little girl we met outside.

After reviewing the menu - I really wanted to try the Violetta but didn't because I just had espresso - we ordered truffles and sampled some of their bars.  Without exaggeration, this is the best chocolate I've ever tasted. The truffle was perfect. All the big name brands don't hold a candle to these folks.  This place has ruined all other chocolates for me.

We'll be back for sure. Highly recommend.

The owner is American and his wife is Peruvian - and his precious little daughter is of color.

I don't believe the race card applies to these people.</review>

I love this place. I try to come at least once a week. Great staff, facilities, and overall experience. I would recommend that if you are coming with a group that you call ahead to ensure that they can fit you in. It's so much fun that they always seem to have at least one station being used.

<review>This was a great way to spend an hour in Lancaster and a good deal, too!
I  went on a Thursday at 3:30 with my fianc√© and we were the only people throwing in there. Ariana, the employee (owner maybe?) helping us, was friendly, personable, and--most importantly--very knowledgeable about how to help first-time axe throwers hit the board. She taught us four different throws to help us figure out which felt the most comfortable and then helped us adjust our footing to make sure the axe stuck in the wooden target after we got the power part down. I hit a few bullseyes, and my fianc√© was hitting them constantly.

< Text>
Wonderful improvement from previous owners. They just recently opened in November 2016 and have so far been succeeding in their business. They inherited the place from a previous family that took poor care of the business and struggled the first month to convince old patrons to come back to the business (i'll admit even I was hesitant, knowing the condition it was previously in), but this new family has done a great job at turning the place around and are clean, not to mention the food is great.

My favorites here are:
Spring Rolls, Chicken Sandwich, the Vermicelli with chicken and eggroll, and their Shrimp or Seafood Pho.< /Text>

<UserId.>101008581620468036960<//UserId.>< Name>
Kevin Reynolds< /Name>
<time>1622686594737<//time><Rating>1<//Rating>< review>
This place has a great selection and most of the staff are super nice. But beware of Dylan, the assistant manager.

So check this: After buying some expensive slab, I go back to pick out the backsplash tile. I was sent to Dylan, who has his own office by the slab yard, to ring me up. I tell him I have a contractor's discount, told him my GC's name, and he nods saying he thinks he knows the guy.

So Dylan is calculating away and when he presents the final bill, I ask if the discount had been applied. Dylan actually says, "I got you, don't worry" and almost winks at me. I handed over my credit card, took the bill home and looked closer. Then I called the store again, asked how much the tile was that I chose and sure enough, Dylan applied no GC discount. I paid retail.

I call Dylan again and said, hey, mistake made. 'Oh, no, don't worry. So sorry. Let me see..." then Dylan tells me to come back for a $59 (and change) refund.

A few weeks later, I'm by the place, stop in and find Dylan at his desk. He kinda/sorta remembers, looks it up and says, "Oh yeah, you get a $22 refund." I reminded him that he told me $59.

Long story short, this guy lied to my face twice in one sentence trying to explain the price difference. He took as long as possible and when all was said and done, I walked out with the $59 refund.

It made me wonder if the owners and managers know this guy is stealing from their customers, boldly lying to them, cheating them out of pennies. But hey, you add up a lot of pennies and you get real money. So maybe that's what the Arizona Tile owners want? Hard to tell. One thing I do know for a fact is that Dylan is a liar, cheat and thief.</review>
